 *** The problem of migraine has become very common
 ye dard kabhi bhi or kahin bhi ho saktaa he
 Although there can be many reasons for migraine, it is also a genetic disease
 matlab, agar aapke ghar main koi migraine kaa pesheynt rah chukaa he to ho saktaa he ki uski ye problem transfar ho jaae
 Migraine causes sharp pain on one side of the head
 is dard ko bardaasht kar paanaa vaaki bahut mushkil he
 Vomiting, dizziness, and feeling tired are the main symptoms of migraine
 migraine kaa dard sir ke ek hisse main hota he isliye ise aam bolchaal main adhakapari bhi kehete hai
 
 migraine ke dard ko kam karne ke liye kai tarah kii davaaiyaan maujuud hai lekin aap chahen to kuch gharelu upaay apanaakar bhi migraine ke dard ko kam kar sakate hai

 There can be many reasons for migraine
 kai baar ye tension kii vajah se ho jaataa he or kai baar hamaari ast-vyast lifestil ke chalate

 2
 Eating fish will also be beneficial

 3

 jo cells ko energy dene kaa kaam karata he

 harley davidson ne haal hi main bharat main 12
 Has introduced a motorcycle worth 80 lakh rupees and also said that the company is considering assembling several models in India, so that customers can get vehicles here at a lower price
 harley davidson india ke prabandh nideshak anup prakaash ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, ham apane dilarship network kaa vistaar kar rahe hai
 We currently have nine showrooms and by the end of this year our 10th showroom will open and next year we will open three more showrooms in Jaipur, Indore and Pune
 tippaniyan He said that the company has decided to increase its presence in second-tier cities, as there is a demand for Harley Davidson motorcycles, which are yet to be known
 prakaash ne kaha, hamen chote shaharon main acchhee maang dikh rahi he
 Asked if Harley Davidson would assemble more models in India to reduce the price, he said, although we do not have any such plans immediately, we will keep this option open to make our products available to customers at a lower price
